TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE
[Part II—Sec. 2
NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
COMMERCIAL TAXES AND REGISTRATION
DEPARTMENT
Notifications under the Indian Stamp Act.
Provisions for the consolidation of duty chargeable in
respect of issue of Policies by the Star Health and
Allied Insurance company Limited through its branches
in the State of Tamil Nadu for certain period under the
Act.
[G.O.(Rt.) No. 71, Commercial Taxes and Registration
(J1), 6th February 2014, ¬î 24, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´ 2045.]
No.II(2)/CTR/208/2014.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 9 of
the Indian Stamp Act, 1899 (Central Act II of 1899), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby provides for the
consolidation of duty of Rs.2,00,000/- (Rupees Two lakh
only) chargeable under the said Act in respect of issue of
policies by the Star health and Allied Insurance Company
Limited, Chennai through its branches in the State of
Tamil Nadu for the period from 1st February 2014 to 31st
March 2014.
Provisions for the consolidation of duty chargeable in
respect of issue of Policies by the Life Insurance
Corporation of India through its P&GS Department,
Divisional  Office for certain period under the Act.
[G.O.(Rt) No.72, Commercial Taxes and Registration (J1),
6th February 2014, ¬î 24, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´ 2045.]
No.II(2)/CTR/209/2014.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 9 of
the Indian Stamp Act, 1899 (Central Act II of 1899), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby provides for the
consolidation of duty of Rs. 20,00,000/- (Rupees Twenty
lakh only) chargeable under the said Act in respect of issue
of policies by Life Insurance Corporation of India through
its P& GS Department Divisional Office for the period from
1st January 2014 to 31st March 2014.
C. JAYARAMAN,
Deputy Secretary to Government.
HIGHWAYS AND MINOR PORTS DEPARTMENT.
Acquisition of Lands.
[G.O.Ms. No. 239, Highways and Minor Ports (HW2),
31st December 2013, ñ£˜èN 16, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´-2044.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/210/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been statistied that the lands specified in the
schedule below have to be acquired for highways Purpose,
to wit for improving and widening of two lane to four lanes
and improvements to Kosasthalayar Bridge Puthur Road at
Km. 0/0–21/0 (SH-51) and it having already been decided
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for
the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or
managed by the Chief Engineer (Construction and
Maintenance), Highways Department and after having
considered the cause shown by the owners or other persons
having interest in the said lands, as the case may be do hereby
publish, the following notice under sub-section 1 of Section 15
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of
2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the  Tamil Nadu
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified
in the schedule below Measuring to an extent of 19380
Square Metres to be the same, a little more or less are
needed for Highways  Purpose, to wit for improving and
widening of two lane to four lanes and improvements to
Kosasthalayar Bridge Puthur Road at K.M.0/0-21/0. (SH-51).
SCHEDULE
Thiruvallur District, Uthukottai Taluk, No. 60 Thandalam
Village.

No. II(2)/HWMP/211/2014-The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the Lands specified in the schedule
below have to be acquired for highways purpose, to formation
of Bypass Road to Tiruttani Town starting from Km 10/4 of
NH 205 and ending at Km. 104/2 of SCKAT Road-SH-58 and
it having already been decided that the entire amount of
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out
of the funds controlled and managed by the Chief Engineer
(Construction and Maintenance), Highways Department, and
after having considered the cause shown by the owners or
other persons having interest in the said lands, as the case
may be, do hereby publish the following notice under
sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu, Highways Act
2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of Tamil Nadu Highways
Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor of Tamil
Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below
measuring to an extent of 11065 Sq. mts. to the same a little
more or less are needed for highways the purpose, to formation
of byposs Road to Tiruttani Town starting from Km 10/4 of
NH 205 and ending at km.104/2 of SCKAT Road-SH-58 in
respect of Devasenapuram Village and Valliammapuram Village
in Tiruttani Taluk, Thiruvallur District.

No. II(2)/HWMP/212/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule
below have to be acquired for highways purpose, to formation
of Bypass Road, to Thiruttani Town starting from Km 10/4 of
NH 205 and ending at km. 104/2 of  SCKAT Road-SH-58 and
it having already been decided that the entire amount of
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out
of the funds controlled or managed by the Chief Engineer
(Construction and Maintenance), Highways Department and
after having considered the cause shown by the owners or
other persons having interest in the said lands, as the case
may be do hereby publish, the following notice under
Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways
Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified
in the schedule below measuring to an extent of 52245
Square Metres to be the same a little more or less are
needed for Highways purpose, to formation of bypass Road
to Tiruttani Town starting from Km 10/4 of NH 205 and
ending at km.104/2 of SCKAT Road-SH-58 at No. 21.
Thiruthani Village and Taluk, Thiruvallur District.

TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE
[Part II—Sec. 2
[G.O. Ms. No. 244, Highways and Minor Ports (HW2),
31st December 2013, ñ£˜èN 16, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´ 2044.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/213/2014—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule
below have to be acquired for highways Purpose, to formation
of Bye-pass Road to Thiruthani Town starting from Km NH
205 and ending at km. 104/2 of SCKAT Road-SH-58 and it
having already been decided that the entire amount of
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out
of the funds controlled or managed by the Chief Engineer
(Construction and Maintenance) Highways Department and after
having considered the cause shown by the owners or other
persons having interest in the said lands, as the case may
be do hereby publish, the following notice under
sub-section 1 of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act,
2001. (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the
schedule below measuring to an extent of 16600 Square
Metres to be the same a little more or less are needed for
Highways Purpose for the formation of Bye-pass Road to
Thiruthani Town starting from NH 205 and ending at
km. 104/2 of SCKAT Road-SH-58 in respect of
Pattabiramapuram Village, Thiruthani Taluk, Thirvallur District.
SCHEDULE
Thiruvallur district, Thiruttani Taluk, No. 22.

[G.O. Ms. No. 245, Highways and Minor Ports (HW2),
31st December 2013, ñ£˜èN 16,
Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´ 2044.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/214/2014.-The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the scheduled
below have to be acquired for highways Purpose, to wit for
improving and widening of two lane to four lane and
improvements to Kosasthalayar Bridge Puthur Road at
Km 0/0- 21/0 (SH-51) and it having already been decided
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for
the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed
by the Chief Engineer (Construction and maintenance),
Highways Dement and after having considered the cause
shown by the owners or other persons having interest in
the said lands, as the case may be do hereby publish, the
following notice under sub-section 1 of Section 15 of the
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001. (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquired the lands specified in the
schedule below measuring to an extent of 33735 Square Metres
to be the same a little more or less are needed for Highways
Purpose, to wit for improving and widening of two lane to four
lane and improvements to Kosasthalayar Bridge Puthur Road
at 0/0 Km 21-0 (SH-51).

No. II(2)/HWMP/218/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands in the schedule below are
required for the purpose of Widening of ECR to six lane from
Thiruvanmiyur to Akkarai it having already been decided that
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands
is to be paid out of the funds controlled and managed by the
Divisional Engineer, Chennai Metropolitan Development Plan,
Division-I, Guindy, Chennai – 32 and after having considered


Feb. 26, 2014]
TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE
295
the cause shown by the owner or other person having interest
in the said lands, as the case may be, do hereby publish the
following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the
Tamil Nadu Highways Act 2001 (TN Act 34/2002)
NOTICE
Under  sub  section  (1)  of  Section  15  of  the  Tamil
Nadu  Highways  Act 2001(TN Act 34/2002), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the
schedule below measuring to an extent of  11445 Sq. metres
to the same, a little more or less required for the purpose
of Widening of ECR to six lane from Thiruvanmiyur to
Akkarai.
The plan of the land under acquisition kept  in the Office
of the Special Deputy Collector (Land Acquisition), Tamil Nadu
Urban Development Project-III, Chennai at Poonamallee and
may be inspected at any time during office hours.

[G.O. (D) No. 298, Highways and Minor Ports (HQ2),

No. II(2)/HWMP/223/2014.—The Governor of Tamil Nadu
having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule
below have to be acquired for Highways purpose for the
formation of By-pass road to Rasipuram town in Namakkal
District and it having already been decided that the entire
amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be
paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Chief Engineer
(Construction & Maintenance), Highways Department,
Chennai-05 after considering the cause shown by the owners
or other persons having interest on the said lands as the case
may be, do hereby publish the following Notice under
sub-section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act,
2001. (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu
Highways Act 2001, (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the
Schedule below admeasuring an extent of 2400 sq.mts of dry
lands to the same, a little more or less needed for the
Highways purpose for the formation of By-pass road to
Rasipuram town in Namakkal District.
The Plan of the lands is kept in the office of the District

HOME PROHIBITION AND EXCISE DEPARTMENT
Amendment to the Tamil Nadu Prohibition Act.
[G.O.Ms.No. 5, Home Prohibition and Excise (III)
7th February 2014.]
No.II(2)/HOPE/228/2014.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by sub-section (1) of Section 18-B of the Tamil Nadu
Prohibition Act, 1937 (Tamil Nadu Act X of 1937), the Governor
of Tamil Nadu hereby makes the following amendments to the
Prohibition and Excise Department Notification No. II(1)/PE/239/
(d)/81, dated the 1st May 1981, pubilished at page 2 of Part
II-Section 1 of the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette
Extraordinary, dated the 1st May 1981, as subsequently
amended:—
AMENDMENTS
In the said Notification, in the Table, in the Annexure to the
entry “Indian Made Foreign Spirits (brand names of which are
specified in the Annexure) other than sacramental wine”.
(i)
under the heading “Ordinary Brands” under the
sub-heading “Thiruvalargal Southern Agrifurane Industries
Limited”, the entry “Haywards Strong Rum” shall be omitted.
(ii)
under the heading “Medium Brands”, under the
sub-heading “Thiruvalargal Southern Agrifurane Industries
Limited”, the following entries shall be omitted, namely:—
“Old Tavern Whisky”,
“Haywards Golconda Brandy”,
John Exshaw Brandy” and
“White Mischief Premium Brandy”

LABOUR AND EMPLOYMENT DEPARTMENT
Notifications under the Industrial Disputes Act.
Declaration of Fertiliser Industry as Public utility Service
for certain period under the Act.
[G.O. (Rt.) No. 64, Labour and Employment (D2),
7th February 2014, Thai 25, Vijaya Thiruvalluvar Aandu,
2045.]
No. II(2)/LE/229/2014.—Whereas, the Governor of Tamil
Nadu is satisfied that public interest requires that the fertiliser
industry should be declared to be a public utility service for
the purposes of the Industrial Disputes Act, 1947 (Central Act
XIV of 1947);
Now, Therefore, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-
clause (vi) of clause (n) of section 2 of the said Act, the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares the fertiliser industry
to be a public utility services for the purposes of the said Act
for a period of six months with effect on and from the date
of publication of this Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government
Gazette.

Earth Moving Equipment like Dumpers, Loaders,
Crawler, Tractors, Coal haulers and excavators as

haulers and excavators’’ should be declared to be a public utility

(Central Act XIV of 1947);

sub-clause (vi) of clause (n) of section 2 of the said Act, the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares the ‘’Industries
Manufacturing and Marketing Earth Moving Equipments like
Dumpers, Loaders, Crawler, Tractors, Coal haulers and

Declaration of Automobile Manufacturing Industry as
Public utility Service for certain period under the Act.
[G.O. (Rt.) No. 67, Labour and Employment (D2),
10th February 2014, Thai 28, Vijaya, Thiruvalluvar Aandu,
2045.]
No. II(2)/LE/231/2014.—Whereas, the Governor of
Tamil Nadu is satisfied that public interest requires that the
Automobile Manufacturing Industry should be declared to be a
public utility service for the purposes of the Industrial Disputes
Act, 1947 (Central Act XIV of 1947);
Now, Therefore, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-
clause (vi) of clause (n) of section 2 read with the proviso
thereto of the said Act, the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby
declares the Automobile Manufacturing Industry to be a public
utility services for the purposes of the said Act for a period
of six months on and from the date of publication of this
Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette.
MOHAN PYARE,
Principal Secretary to Government.
